AboutText=[[
Hello guys. Although this isn't my first trainer(actually my 2nd), it is my biggest.
This trainer should work for both the Gold and Standard Edition of the Steamworks
version of Resident Evil 5.
Please, before using this, backup your save file at this directory:
C:\Program Files (x86)\Steam\userdata\205566341\21690\remote
Then, download Wilsonso's patch from here:
http://www.mediafire.com/download/6cymabc64sm8ani/
Afterwards, install the Prerequisite and Crash Fix inside the nativePC folder to both of these directories:
C:\Program Files (x86)\Steam\SteamApps\common\Resident Evil 5\nativePC
C:\Program Files (x86)\Steam\SteamApps\common\Resident Evil 5\nativePC_MT

This trainer took a very long time to make, so please do not steal credit for this for yourself.
Also, whatever you do with this, it is on you, not me. Otherwise, enjoy the tool!

DISCLAIMER!
THE TRAINER AUTHOR, EXPRESSLY DISCLAIMS ANY WARRANTY, EXPRESSED
OR IMPLIED, AND ACCEPTS NO RESPONSIBILITY FOR THE QUALITY OR RELIABILITY
OF THE TRAINER OFFERED. THE AUTHOR SHOULD ACCEPT NO RESPONSIBILITY

]]

First and foremost, I'd like to thank both God and his son Jesus Christ for giving me the knowledge and patience to make this trainer.

CharacterHelp=[[
The character change cheat WILL freeze you or any other client who joins you(or you join) unless both they
and you have Wilsonso's patch installed. Also, for the Invincibility... It works for everything except things that skip the Dying Counter.
Also, if both players get downed at once, the game will call an automatic game over, so don't shoot both of yourselves with a rocket at the same time!
Also, there sometimes appears to be a bit of a delay between the updating of health in-game(due to around 10 different pointers controlling the value)
so Invincibility might not save you at times(although 90% of the time, it will)
]]

InventoryHelp=[[
Only use the item editors if an item in in the slot you plan to edit. Else, it'll act kind of funny.
In order for the changes to take effect, you must click move on the item after you edit it, and move it back to the slot you edited.
Damage Mod will either give your gun's damage a nice upgrade or make it a worthless peashooter(different for different guns)
Any item that says throwable likely either does no damage or only does damage to you. Still, it's a random item you can enjoy chucking
around.
Any item that says must shoot will actually deal damage to enemies, but must be shot after being thrown to trigger the effect.
Barry's Samurai Edge will crash anyone(whether they join you or you join them) who does not have the Gold Edition. Do not equip
this if they have Standard.
]]

UDF1.show()
getAutoAttachList().add("re5dx9.exe")

addresslist=getAddressList()

function CloseClick()
  closeCE()
  return caFree
end

UDF1.OnClose = CloseClick

function CEComboBox11Select(sender)
t = createTimer(UDF1.CEComboBox11, true)
t.Interval = 100
t.OnTimer = function(sender)
t.Enabled = UDF1.CEComboBox11.OnSelect

   index = UDF1.CEComboBox11.ItemIndex
   if index == -1 then return end;
   if index == 0 then
      writeInteger("[re5dx9.exe+00DA21B8]+23318",0)
   elseif index == 1 then
      writeInteger("[re5dx9.exe+00DA21B8]+23318",1)
   elseif index == 2 then
      writeInteger("[re5dx9.exe+00DA21B8]+23318",2)
   elseif index == 3 then
      writeInteger("[re5dx9.exe+00DA21B8]+23318",3)
   elseif index == 4 then
      writeInteger("[re5dx9.exe+00DA21B8]+23318",4)
   end
      end
end

  memoryrecord_freeze(CheatEntry)
